    903 <a href="#l884" class="line" id="l884">    884</a> &lt;/a&gt; 5. Back-end: Well, maybe this is kind of huge for me. I&amp;#39;ve been doing front-end stuff for a while and my backend skills are getting pretty bad. My experience working with [Express](https://expressjs.com/es/) and [Adonis](https://adonisjs.com/) was pretty good, but it was simple things. I don&amp;#39;t know anything about databases too. So, yeah. Maybe I&amp;#39;ll buy a course from [Udemy](https://www.udemy.com/) for it.
    904 <a href="#l885" class="line" id="l885">    885</a>  6. CSS Art: Yes, another art stuff. All the [beautiful CSS art that is on codepen](https://codepen.io/tag/css-art) makes me want to do something similar. I&amp;#39;m not sure what exactly but some 3D CSS animations are on my eye.
    905 <a href="#l886" class="line" id="l886">    886</a>  7. Being fluent in Esperanto and learning more about romantic languages: Duolingo and [Lernu](https://lernu.net/) are my best friends here.
